< Text>
Seven different employees came up to me at this small store. I wore a mask, I waited in line without complaints, I washed my hands, and I had antibacterial gel ready and available on my keychain.

I had three employees try to ask me what I wanted before I had even entered the store because they wanted me to be checked out without entry. They let everyone else in with a smile.

A woman and her daughter who were ahead of me were greeted kindly; no soap was given to them to wash their hands.

They were not harassed when they went inside, and they were given time to look at items.

I used to love LUSH.

LUSH products used to be perfect for Christmas gifts in my book. Also, a great Stock.

I have used the Ayesha mask and got my family hooked onto Dream Cream.

I just wanted to look around at their new stuff and buy presents.

My experience here was Discriminatory and Revolting. I will not be buying LUSH ever again.< /Text>

First a little dental backstory for me. I'm one of those "lucky" people that has to self medicate before a dentist appointment because of anxiety. At the dentist I went to before Sequoia Dental it took a full year of regular appointments for me to finally be able to be seen without the use of nitrous. It isn't the pain so much as it is the noises associated with the dentist's office and the feeling of vulnerability  that happens when the exam chair gets reclined back. Now that brings me to my appointment yesterday at Sequoia Dental. It was an emergency appointment as I was experiencing acute pain from one of my crowns. The staff was very nice and was very closely following social distancing recommendations. Xrays were a breeze and the first doctor I met with was a nice older gentleman. He said I'd need a root canal, new post and a crown. I was tempted to just have him pull it because of the cost but other than needing some TLC the tooth is a good one so I opted to go through with the root canal, post and crown. The next doctor I met with is the reason I'm taking the time to write this review. He was amazing. I felt no pain, nada, 0, zilch. The shots to numb me didn't even hurt. Between getting through the shots pain free and him continuously checking in on me I was more comfortable than I have ever been at a dentist. Thank you Dr. Bui.< /text>

She also offered me use of the complimentary dolly - something I was unaware of when moving in. Definitely an AMAZING team member.

Hannah has a wonderful spirit and jovial attitude. When a unit I reserved online was given to another person before I moved in, she made sure to address not only the concern but also to make sure I was taken care of right away. She worked with me the same day to make sure everything was addressed and taken care of the exact same day, resolving the concern to the best of her ability.

STAFF HERE IS AWESOME! You can't pay someone enough for their customer service!

Storage wise:

- Super Safe location (which is important for me, as I left another storage because it was not as safe)

- Very Clean

- Daily Hours to visit your storage are great too (6a-9p) Longer than I've seen at others.

Definitely consider keeping your items here. My wife did about 5 years ago when we needed it, and it's still a quality storage even today.<//Review>

< text>
Wow - this place is the real deal - owned by a Sicilian couple - she's in the kitchen and he's out front hosting.  Charming restaurant with indoor & outdoor seating off the main drag and away from the crowds.  Everything was perfect - the Flanghina wine, the Burrata caprese with roasted and chilled tomatoes that were delicious - only misstep is that we didn't get the amazing warm bread until after the Caprese was taken away - would have loved to wipe the plate clean with it!  I had the Branzino filet piccata, which was perfectly cooked & beyond perfection.  It came with an artichoke, sun dried tomato and spinach salad - lovely side dish.  Husband asked for something fruitti di mare & they made him an incredible spaghetti with white wine garlic sauce and shrimp.  Such a simple dish, but so easy to mess it up - tasted like some of the best we've had on the Amalfi Coast.  Great friendly service.  So happy to find this - we normally travel to Italy once or twice a year for the food, so until we can go back... we've found a wonderful substitute!<//text>

< Text>
There are many good restaurants in Palm Springs, but a few stand out as truly exceptional - Il Giardino is among the elite.
Unlike many places, they don't need to try to be special because they understand that great food is about having the best ingredients prepared flawlessly.
Take their calamari appetizer for example. It is not breaded and deep-fried, it is simply prepared with the red sauce but tender, juicy, and flavorful unlike almost any other calamari you will find.
their entrees are likewise delicious and perfectly prepared. I recently had the eggplant Parmesan special and the eggplant was tender and flavorful along with a delicious simple red sauce. This is what Italian food is meant to be.</Text>

<time>1582055473461< /time><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
What an incredible find. Gabby's is known for their Mexican cuisine. Did you know that their Italian dishes are out of this world? We absolutely loved our Italian plates and the service was perfect. 5 Stars for the red sauce dish. We were seated towards the back where it is a little quieter and we felt as if we had VIP service. < Text>
I had the worst dining experience in my life tonight due to an extremely defensive and rude hostess.  I made it a point of mine to regularly order takeout and patronize the Yasai to do my part to support local business, especially plant-based restaurants, which are going through a rough time during COVID. I even celebrated my 37th birthday here in November and my waiter was nice enough to store my birthday cake in their refrigerator. In all, I would estimate that I've patronized this restaurant roughly 20+ times. However, today was unlike any other time that I tried to order food. My date and I arrived at 6:30 PM at the Yasai on India Street and asked for a table for 2. For instance, the inside of the restaurant was full, which is a violation of COVID restrictions. Nevertheless, the outside only had one table occupied with the other 6 or so others open. The hostess said, "We don't have any seating available." I then asked how many reservations were booked and whether there was an opening soon. The hostess said, "We have an opening at 7:30." I then asked, "It's 6:30 now. Did anyone no show because there's seven seats available based on the tables." She said, "We can't be congested due to COVID." I then said, "Aren't the tables outside already socially distanced?" Then my date said, "We'll take the 7:30 time slot." The hostess then said, "Actually, we have the right to deny service. You can eat elsewhere. Have a good night!" I then asked if I could speak to the manager. Then she walked away. She comes back about 2 mins later and says, "My manager is unavailable." I said I'll wait. She then leaves again to go to the kitchen in the back of the restaurant where I can see her talking to a chef in a white hat. The hostess then returns to us in the front and says, "My manager said I'm the supervisor." I then said, "So now you're the manager or are you the supervisor? How do you supervise yourself? My date then asks her what her name is. The hostess says, "I don't have to tell you my name." Then walks away yet again! At this point it was apparent to me that the staff here provided no information to the public nor was there any visible food licensing permits, legible COVID reopen plan, or business permits. In short, there is no point of contact name or contact information displayed for patrons to even report complaints such as this, so the hostess refusing to even provide her name and her failure to bring a manager to hear my concerns is apparently business as usual. Therefore, I will never spend another dime here and encourage you to do the same.</Text>

<text>I came here as a party of 12 (big family) and was seated within 30 minutes despite the dinner rush (6 pm on a Saturday). We were greeted with chips and salsa at the table, which carried a hint of spice, but was still enjoyable for the kids. I ordered the Cadillac Margarita, and my wife had the Anta's Spicy Margarita, both of which were quite enjoyable (the spicy margarita certainly lives up to it's name). I had the Fajitas, and with choices of chicken, New York Steak, or grilled shrimp (you can mix for a fee) I opted for a mix of steak and shrimp. The food, drinks, and staff were all exceptional. What truly made this place stand out to me was the diversity of selection. Unlike most restaurants who have outdoor parking lot tented dinning , Anita's has a real outdoor covered patio with tiled floors and heater lamps. My friend and I celebrated her birthday with frozen margaritas during happy hour. Afterwards we warmed up with chicken tortilla soup for me and albondigas (meatball) soup for the birthday girl. There are 3 sizes to choose from; a cup, small bowl or large bowl, and we both went with the small bowl. It was perfect for a light but filling dinner, not to mention delicious! Our server was quick and very friendly.  I'll definitely be going back.< /Review>< Pictures>

Just moved into the area and checking out the local eats. Anita's was recommended to us. We loved the look and feel of the place as soon as we walked in. The decor' is really inviting and sets off a great vibe for a fun dining experience. We ordered large margaritas from the bar until our table was ready. We liked the drinks, but found the almost 14.00 drinks a bit much in price. Our bar tab was almost as much as our meals. Our server and bartender were pleasant. Our 4 dinners were all very good (Carnitas, grilled fish, chicken enchiladas and grilled shrimp), but served with traditional sides - beans and rice. The cost for the meals was a bit high considering the sides in my opinion. Overall, it was a good evening. We sat on the patio. It was a bit loud, but comfortable on a summer night.<//text>

<Text>My sister and I had plans to go have breakfast at a place right by Anita's before my train.  Unfortunately we ran into a full parking lot and a wait.  So, we decided on Anita's instead. < Review>
Really enjoy the scene here, though it gets pretty busy during the weekend! The cooks here are really amazing at what they do and the waiters are fabulous! Our waiter was on top of it! Along with the man serving our food. Delicious food. Great service. And a nice space. The only downfall is because there are so many people who enjoy this place, weekend wait times can stretch and there isn't too much seating for hungry customers. < user_name>
Cory Baehr</user_name>
<Text>Anita's has finally moved to their beautiful new location.  This is a local favorite and a place we visit frequently.   Very pleased with the new location even though it is further from home in South Oceanside and area that is growing by leaps and bounds with wonderful new restaurants, small shops and coffee houses.   I love this place so I will give them a little more time to work out the rough edges.   They are struggling a little with trying to get help, the kitchen staff needs to stabilize.  Working out the kinks is difficult even for a place that has been in business for years.  Turnover in the restaurant business is a big problem currently from fast food all the way up the food chain.   A few friends have complained that they increased prices but $10.95 is still a bargain for a large plate of sour cream chicken enchiladas, beans, rice, tortilla's and salsa, my favorite.  With the expense of relocating a small price increase is certainly understandable.  Wait staff is great and apologetic.  We love you, Anita's and we will keep coming back until you are back to your five star rating.  We love to support local, family owned businesses. Be sure to have a margarita!!< /Text><Resp>None<//Resp></record>

< Review>
We've been going to the ORIGINAL Anita's for 40 years, and the new location came with great disappointment! Nothing tasted like it used to. The service was horrible, but the food was the worst Mexican food we've ever eaten! Our two boys ordered the 'Chicken Tenders' and they were served frozen Tyson Dino nuggets. The chicken in the soft tacos was bland, dry, and just gross tasting. Our daughters chimichanga was supposed to be beef and bean, instead it was some kind of inedible dog food. The shrimp and steak fajitas was an insult to steak and shrimp fajitas. Very dry flavorless shrimp, and tiny little worm like strings of meat. None of us ever want to go back to this place, which is so incredibly sad because it's been a family favorite for 40 years!!!! What happened? New owners? New kitchen staff? New menu? Honestly I wouldn't even feed my dog the "food" they serve here. Not worth the one star review.</Review>
